62nd Meeting of the Executive Yuan

At the 62nd meeting of the Executive Yuan on the 25th, Tan Yankai, He Yingqin, Kong Xiangxi, Sun Ke, Liu Ruiheng, Jiang Menglin, and Wang Zhengting were present. Chairman Tan Yankai discussed the following matters: (1) The Office of the National Government forwarded a letter regarding attention to the selection of county magistrates, which was resolved by the 68th State Affairs Conference to be referred to the Executive Yuan for appropriate measures. It was resolved to refer it to the Ministry of Interior for appropriate planning. (2) The Central Political Conference forwarded a letter regarding Committee Member Yu Youren's proposal to request the allocation of 1 million in cash in the shortest possible time to charitable organizations such as the Famine Relief Committee to provide relief in Shaanxi Province to save the disaster victims. If immediate arrangements are not possible, please allocate 300,000 to 500,000 yuan first to alleviate the urgent need. It was resolved to refer it to the Executive Yuan for handling and resolved to refer it to the Ministry of Finance for the allocation of 300,000 yuan. (3) The Central Political Conference forwarded a letter regarding the proposal of four committee members, including Zhang Renjie, that the National Games will open soon, requiring a large amount of funds. Please approve a subsidy of 50,000 yuan to support the event. It was resolved to refer it to the Executive Yuan and resolved to subsidize 20,000 yuan. (4) The Ministry of Industry and Commerce forwarded a letter stating that the 14th International Labor Conference has been confirmed to be held in Geneva, Switzerland on June 10 this year. The ministry has drafted the relevant measures for our country to send representatives to attend the conference, and has also submitted a budget for review and referral. It was resolved to approve the original proposal and refer the funds to the Ministry of Finance for allocation. (5) The Ministry of Transportation submitted two draft laws, the Shipping Law and the Ship Registration Law, for review and referral to the Legislative Yuan for deliberation. It was resolved to send them to the Legislative Yuan for deliberation. (6) The Ministry of Transportation proposed submitting the Regulations for the Levy of Additional Contributions for Shipping Schools for review and record. It was resolved to approve the filing.

82nd Meeting of the Legislative Yuan

The Legislative Yuan held its 82nd meeting at 8:00 AM today (the 25th). Committee members Jiao Yitang, Shi Shangkuan, Chen Zhaoying, Lin Bin, Ma Yinchu, Tao Xuan, Shao Yuanchong, Sun Jingya, Lou Tongsun, Wu Shangying, Zhang Zhihan, Wang Yongbin, Liu Guantun, Zhuang Songfu, Lu Zhonglin, Liu Jixue, Luo Ding, Zeng Jie, Wei Tingsheng, Zhang Fengjiu, Fu Bingchang, Chen Changheng, Liu Kejun, Zhu Hezhong, Zheng Kaichen, Wei Huai, and 26 others were present. Chairman Hu Hanmin discussed the following matters: (1) Deliberation on the draft Implementing Regulations of the Negotiable Instruments Law, it was resolved to refer it to the Commercial Law Drafting Committee for review. (2) The Executive Yuan requested an interpretation of the ambiguities in the Trade Union Law, it was resolved to refer it to the Labor Law Drafting Committee for review. (3) Amendment to the Organizational Law of the Ministry of Agriculture and Mining, it was resolved to refer it to the Legal System Committee for review. (4) Committee members of this Yuan, Jiao Yitang, Wang Yongbin, Ma Yinchu, and others reported on the review of the draft organizational regulations for the Provincial and Regional Civil Service Examination Committees, it was resolved to approve the review report and that the organizational regulations for the Provincial and Regional Civil Service Examination Committees should be discussed later.

Zhang Jingjiang Goes to Fenghua to Meet Chiang

Ningbo correspondence, Zhejiang Provincial Government Chairman Zhang Jingjiang, upon hearing that Chairman Chiang had returned to his hometown to sweep the tombs, specially crossed the river to Shao yesterday (the 23rd) afternoon, crossed the Cao'e River this morning, and took a special train to Ningbo, arriving at the station around 9:00 AM. He then rode with Ningbo Mayor Yang Ziyi in a Yinfeng Motor Road car to Fenghua Xikou to meet with Chairman Chiang and personally present everything.

After Chairman Chiang arrived in Ningbo on the Chutai warship on the morning of the 22nd, he took his own car directly to his family home in Wenchanggé, Xikou, Fenghua. More than 300 students from the Wuling Primary School (founded by Chairman Chiang) welcomed him at the train station. At 11:00 AM, a welcoming conference was held in the school's auditorium. Then Chairman Chiang and his wife, accompanied by engineer Weng, inspected the newly built school buildings before returning to their family home for lunch. Yesterday (the 23rd) at around 9:00 AM, Chairman Chiang, accompanied by his wife, Madam Soong Meiling, and acting Minister of the Navy Chen Shaokuan, visited Xuebao Temple. They returned to Xikou at 4:00 PM.

Coastal Zhejiang Police Wipe Out Large Group of Pirates

The areas of Shangxia Dachen in Wenling County, which belongs to the Taizhou Prefecture of Zhejiang Province, are surrounded by the sea on all sides and have long been a stronghold for notorious pirates like Yin Xiaoyan and Jiang Dougao. The local residents have been in contact with them for so long that they have become accustomed to and assimilated with them. Therefore, every time the water police station sent teams to suppress the pirates, the residents always claimed that there were no pirates and everything was peaceful. In reality, the people were mixed with the pirates, making it impossible to distinguish them. This time, Wang Wenhan, the commander of the Offshore Water Police Bureau and concurrently the Anti-Piracy Commander of the four prefectures, recognizing the unrest caused by pirates in the Taizhou waters, specially dispatched Inspector Tang Lun, together with the 5th Regiment of the Zhijiao Security Force, to supervise the Haijing and Yongping patrol ships, as well as the 2nd, 6th, and 7th water patrol teams and the Security Force student company and special task company, to launch a two-pronged attack. One route, led by Inspector Tang and Regiment Commander Zhu, supervised the Haijing ship, the 2nd and 6th water patrol teams, and one platoon of the student company, to suppress the pirates at Guandi'ao in Shang Dachen. The other route, led by Inspector Ke Dejia and Deputy Regiment Commander Lü, supervised the Yongping ship, the 7th water patrol team, and the Security Force special task company, to suppress the pirates at Shangtou'ao in Shang Dachen. Both groups landed simultaneously at dawn on the 17th of this month. The pirates on the lookout immediately scattered and returned to their lairs to report. The soldiers and police bravely advanced and encountered a group of more than a hundred pirates at Bantianfei. They attacked each other and held their ground for four hours. Sixty to seventy pirates were killed on the spot, but they still resisted stubbornly. The Haijing ship then circled behind the pirates and bombarded them with cannons. The remaining pirates lost their courage and were forced into the sea, with none escaping. On the morning of the 18th, a search was conducted in the mountains and valleys of Puli in Xia Dachen. A temple was found with its doors locked, which seemed suspicious. The locks were broken, and the temple was searched. Unexpectedly, gunfire suddenly erupted. Pirate leaders Yin Xiaoyan, Jiang Dougao, Xiao Wude, and others, along with more than ten guards, were hidden inside. As soon as they saw the police and soldiers, they vigorously fired with wooden-shell guns. Although the police and soldiers surrounded the temple and attacked fiercely, the temple's stone walls were solid and difficult to destroy. Fire was then used to surround and burn the temple, and all the pirate leaders inside, including Yin Xiaoyan, were burned to death. The pirate leader Jiang Dougao rushed out through the fire and was also killed on the spot. Afterwards, the bodies were examined, and it was found that the pirate leader Yin Xiaoyan was wearing a bulletproof vest, with steel fragments still remaining in the ashes. According to statistics, more than a hundred notorious pirate leaders and pirates were wiped out in Shangxia Dachen this time. More than thirty rifles and more than ten wooden-shell pistols were seized, and more than thirty refugees were rescued. After this severe suppression, even if there are small groups of pirates in Taiwan, it will be easier to eliminate them.

Excerpts from Wang Boling's Talk After Returning to the Province

Mr. Wang Boling arrived in the province the day before yesterday. Yesterday morning, he attended the provincial government's memorial service and the provincial committee meeting. I then visited his private residence and had the following conversation with Mr. Wang: (Question) Mr., what were the results of your mission to Yunnan? (Answer) Yunnan is far from the central government, and there is a lack of understanding of the situation. My trip did not achieve much in terms of the central government's tasks, and there are some things that are not convenient to announce at this time. However, since my arrival in Yunnan, Yunnan has truly become the Yunnan of the central government. This is something I can report. (Question) How long were you in Yunnan? (Answer) A full six months. I repeatedly wanted to return east, but the central government did not allow it. By the time the Third Plenary Session opened, I was still on my way back in the South China Sea. (Question) What is the situation in Annam (Vietnam)? (Answer) The late Premier's Three Principles of the People have taken deep root in the hearts of the people. The awakening of small and weak nations is an unstoppable trend. Therefore, the French paid special attention to my passing through Annam, and the French ambassador raised concerns with the central government, saying that General Wang Boling's passage through Vietnam should not involve any revolutionary actions. When I arrived in Haiphong on my return journey, there was an independence movement in Annam. The party headquarters originally asked me to hold a meeting and give a speech, but it could not be held. (Question) What is the strength of the military in Yunnan? (Answer) Two divisions can be deployed. If the central government gives the order, they can be mobilized immediately. (Question) Will you be stationed in the province permanently from now on? (Answer) The living conditions in Yunnan are too poor. I rushed back to Beijing to attend the conference. I recently suffered from a toothache and need to rest a little. I also need to make a trip to the capital to report everything to the Chairman. Tomorrow I will attend the farewell party at the Construction Department. In the afternoon, I will return to Yangzhou to visit my elderly mother. I have been running around for national affairs for half a year and have not dared to attend to my personal duty of serving my parents. I feel very uneasy about this. (Question) When will the construction of the Xiong Martyr's Memorial Hall in Yangzhou begin? (Answer) I must promote this matter when I return to Yangzhou. Fundraising from all parties has reached 30,000 yuan, which is enough to start construction. (Question) Have you completed the handover at the Construction Department? (Answer) Because of my trip to Yunnan, the construction of roads could not be implemented. I still feel regretful about this. However, fortunately, there is still one million yuan left in the construction funds for the counties, and the department's funds still have a principal and interest of more than 500,000 yuan. In the future, Director Sun can implement the original plan step by step, which can still compensate for my aspirations. As we talked to this point, other guests came to visit, so I took my leave and departed.

Reasons for the Influx of Japanese Fish in Quanzhou

Xiamen Correspondence: The Japanese are invading the fishing grounds along the coast of Fujian, and recently they have been selling their frozen fresh fish in Quanzhou, which has greatly affected the fishing industry in Quanzhou. Fishermen from various coastal counties have united to form a Fisheries Congress to discuss ways to resist this. According to an investigation by the Fisheries Union, the intrusion of frozen fish from Taiwan into Quanzhou is due to Jiang Daqing, a Taiwanese who came to Quanzhou last August and organized the Minnan Fisheries Company, claiming to revitalize the Chinese fishing industry. In reality, he specializes in hiring motorboats to transport frozen fish from Taiwan to Quanzhou for sale. At the same time, he also leads Japanese fishing vessels to fish in the waters near Quanzhou. As a result, Jiang can obtain Taiwanese fish at low cost, and the fish caught by Japanese vessels in the waters off Quanzhou are also sold by Jiang in Quanzhou. Therefore, he can manipulate the market price of fresh fish in Quanzhou. The company has three motorboats, "Minnan No. 1," "Minnan No. 2," and "Rongfa 98," each capable of carrying 600 to 800 piculs. They sell an average of 300 piculs of fish per day, with each picul priced at 30 to 40 yuan. Relying on their status as registered residents, they can evade taxes. Jiang is very active in Taiwan, and it is said that the Governor-General of Taiwan has given him a bonus of 10,000 yuan. This shows that Jiang's arrival actually contains the mission of the Japanese to invade the fishing grounds and fish market of Fujian Province. Since Jiang profited, Quanzhou merchants Su Dabing, He Danian, Cai Ruifang, and others envied him and also jointly formed the Huanan Company to transport frozen fish directly from Taiwan to Quanzhou for sale. Later, the Quanzhou Fish Guilds Xiesheng, Heyi, and Shunxing also jointly formed a company and hired the Japanese vessel Xirong Maru to transport fish from Taiwan. A few fishmongers in Quanzhou, Zeng Shitou and Mao Hui, also formed the Minxing Company to transport fish from Taiwan. As a result, the Japanese plan to invade the fresh fish market in Quanzhou gradually succeeded. Since June and July, Quanzhou has been flooded with frozen fish, and our country's fishing industry, which adheres to the law, has suffered a setback. Moreover, the Taiwanese fish that come to Quanzhou are mostly bream, whale sharks, and various small fish. It is difficult to effectively freeze larger fish. The fishing boats sail and the fish stalls store the fish for more than two weeks. After arriving in Quanzhou, the fish merchants' freezing equipment is not complete, and the fish often thaws and rots internally, which is also very unhygienic.

Since the coastal fishermen of Quanzhou united to form a Fisheries Union, they have been proceeding with resistance after filing with the Jinjiang Finger Committee. The first step was to send letters to the associations, ordering all fish merchants not to transport Taiwanese fish. The second step was to raise funds to organize a fishery cooperative, purchase fishing boats, and set up freezing cabinets to catch and store fish using new methods to avoid natural elimination. The first step has gradually achieved results, and the amount of frozen fish in Quanzhou has decreased in recent weeks. The second step is also being actively prepared. (March 21st)

Continued Trial of Ge Jianshi Case in Jiangsu High Court

Defendant Requests That Miao Bin Be Summoned for Confrontation

The case of Ge Jianshi, former Executive Committee Member and Propaganda Director of the Jiangsu Provincial Party Headquarters, Ni Bi, Executive Committee Member, Gu Ziyang, Executive Committee Member and Training Department Director, Wang Zhiren, Training Department Staff, Gu Shuyin, General Affairs Section Staff, Chen Baixin, Propaganda Department Staff, Ge Shangde, Editorial Section Clerk, and others, on suspicion of reactionary activities, was continued today (the 25th) in the First Tribunal of the High Court. Witnesses Chen Jianmin, Yao Chengwen, and Wu Yucang were summoned, along with defense attorneys Wu Chengyu, Lu Xiangru, Chen Liren, and Xu Bingcheng. Judge Lin Dawen, Prosecutor Du Fuyue, and Clerk Zhu Xiongwu opened the trial at 2:10 PM, examining each person one by one. The hearing concluded at 3:15 PM. The details of each person's testimony are recorded below in order:

Gu Ziyang: The judge asked about the letters of accusation from Zhang Zhihui, Wang Dechun, Huang Zhenya, and others. The Civil Affairs Department has sent the original letters. Take a look at them. Gu replied, "I don't know Zhang Zhihui. I don't even know if he exists. He said that Duan Muzhen went to Xuzhou on my orders to convene a Communist Party meeting, but I didn't send him there. I don't know if he went or not. Duan Muzhen was on a mission from the Provincial Party Headquarters to arrest one or two hundred communists. The communists hated him the most. This letter of accusation is probably fabricated by the communists. It's also possible." The judge asked, "Look at the original letters from Wang Dechun and Huang Zhenya again." Gu replied, "If these people are real, why don't they list their addresses? The Civil Affairs Department didn't clarify this either. Under these circumstances, it's probably fabricated by Miao Bin to frame people. What exactly happened? Please summon Miao Bin for confrontation."

Witness Yao Chengwen: The judge asked, "Are you related to Ge Shangde?" Yao replied, "No." The judge asked, "Is Ge Shangde's reply to your letter correct?" Yao replied, "Yes, it's a reply to the letter I gave him." The judge asked, "Why did you give him a letter?" Yao replied, "Because at that time, the Taicang Supervisory Committee was falsely accused by the Executive Committee. The supervisors wanted to file a counter-suit against them. I was instructed to draft a statement of appeal. I wrote a letter to Ge Shangde in my personal capacity, asking him if he wanted to file a counter-suit." The judge asked, "Does the 'untimely moment' mentioned in the letter, 'postpone the launch,' refer to the counter-suit?" Yao replied, "Yes."

Ge Shangde: The judge asked, "Is what the witness said correct?" Ge replied, "Yes. Wu Yucang has also arrived now."

Witness Wu Yucang: The judge asked, "What position do you currently hold?" Wu replied, "Taicang County Party Reorganization Committee Member." The judge asked, "Are you related to Ge Shangde?" Wu replied, "No." The judge asked, "What position did you hold before?" Wu replied, "Taicang County Supervisory Committee Member." The judge asked, "Have you ever been accused to the Provincial Party Headquarters?" Wu replied, "I have been accused to the Provincial Party Headquarters many times by the Executive Committee." The judge asked, "Did you file a counter-suit?" Wu replied, "I also filed a few counter-suits." The judge asked, "Did you ever ask Yao Chengwen to write a letter?" Wu replied, "I asked him to draft a submission for appeal to higher authorities. As for his communication with Ge Shangde about the counter-suit, I didn't know at the time, but I remember that he later told me about it." The judge asked, "Have you seen the contents of Ge Shangde's letter to Yao Chengwen?" Wu replied, "I haven't seen it in detail yet, but I was detained in the Taicang County Public Security Bureau and subjected to torture due to being framed by the Executive Committee. The Public Security Bureau Chief once told me about it." The judge asked, "Does the 'untimely moment' mentioned in Ge Shangde's letter, 'postpone the launch,' refer to the Supervisory Committee's counter-suit against the Executive Committee?" Wu replied, "Ge Shangde's letter to Yao Chengwen was at the time of the Taicang Supervisory Committee's counter-suit. Moreover, judging from the tone of the letter, the court should understand."

Ge Shangde: The judge asked, "Is what Wu Yucang said correct?" Ge replied, "Yes. Regarding this letter, please pay attention to two points. One is that there were indeed disputes in the Taicang County Party Headquarters. The second is that the letter refers to internal disputes within the Taicang Party Headquarters. As long as you look at the context, you can understand. This letter has no reactionary suspicion whatsoever."

Ge Jianshi: The judge asked, "Is what the two comrades said correct?" Ge replied, "Correct." Ni Bi: The judge asked, "Regarding the evidence, it has been investigated. Do you have any requests for further investigation? Regarding the Shi Hanqing matter mentioned in the previous hearing, it was said that you were close to him." Ni replied, "How do you define 'close'? What is the legal meaning of that? What is the basis for the fact of being close? It can't be based on what Miao Bin said. That can't be evidence." The judge asked, "Do you know Shi Hanqing?" Ni replied, "He is a county party committee member. I am a provincial party committee member. Of course, there is a relationship of subordination in terms of duties, but there is no personal relationship." The judge asked, "Is there anything else you want to request for investigation?" Ni replied, "Since Miao Bin became the Director of the Civil Affairs Department of Jiangsu Province, his despicable conduct has been widely known. All party members and the people of the province hate him to the bone. I was a member of the Provincial Party Headquarters. The Provincial Party Headquarters is in a position to supervise the administrative organs. Therefore, we often pointed out his erroneous measures, so he harbors resentment towards us and retaliates under the guise of suspicion. When the prosecutor opened the investigation hearing for the first time, Miao Bin accused us of ten counts, and the prosecutor said that there was evidence, but it was not sent. I immediately said to the prosecutor, 'If there is evidence, and we have been arrested and detained in Zhenjiang for a month, why isn't it sent?' The prosecutor said, 'His official document said that there must be evidence.' Now the court has sent a letter to urge him to produce it. Later, at the second investigation hearing, more than twenty days had passed, that is, it was almost two months since we were arrested, and the evidence had not yet been sent. It was not sent until after the indictment, around the end of February. At this time, it had been three months since we were arrested. After repeated urging from the court, this kind of thing was finally sent. Among them, dozens of absurd words were listed. The only one that is related to the defendant is that I am close to the famous reorganizationist Shi Hanqing. The dates of these copied documents are all between October and November of last year, that is, before we were arrested. Why was this thing not sent until three months later, and after the court had repeatedly urged it? It can be seen that there is a lot of suspicion of forgery and framing under the guise of suspicion, so I want to ask the court to summon him to the court for confrontation, so that the truth can be revealed. Even if the court does not adopt the evidence he said, in order to clarify the facts, the defendant must also request that he be summoned to the court for confrontation to show the truth." The judge asked, "Did Shi Hanqing live in the Provincial Party Headquarters in Zhenjiang, or did he live in your house? Is that true?" Ni replied, "I lived in the Jinshan Temple monastery in Zhenjiang, far away from the Provincial Party Headquarters. I was just a temporary resident in the temple and had no family there. That is very wrong."

Wang Zhiren: The judge asked, "Are you and Lu Yinquan from the same hometown and classmates?" Wang replied, "Yes, but we were classmates several years ago." The judge asked, "After Lu Yinquan left the Provincial Party Headquarters, did you have any contact with him?" Wang replied, "Since he left the Provincial Party Headquarters, there has been no contact." The judge asked, "Was this time the only time you sent him a letter? Is there any other political relationship?" Wang replied, "There is no other relationship. I just advised him to send a few dollars home every month to support his parents."

Gu Shuyin: The judge asked, "Do you have a lot of contact with Fang Yuanmin?" Gu replied, "Fang Yuanmin came to work in the Training Department of the Provincial Party Headquarters in the 18th year [of the Republic of China], and I came to work in the Training Department of the Provincial Party Headquarters before the 17th year. Not only is there no contact, but I don't even know him. Since working in the same department, apart from a brief meeting due to work-related matters, there has been no contact at all." Chen Baixin: The judge asked, "Are you related to Wang Bochun?" Chen replied, "Regarding this point, the defendant has repeatedly explained in detail in court. Due to colleagues, we know each other, but there is no so-called contact." The judge asked, "Regarding the evidence, is there any request for investigation?" Chen replied, "No, because the matter is very clear. The so-called contact is very vague and not worth investigating at all."

Attorney Chen Liren stated, "The Director of the Civil Affairs Department replied to your court with copied documents and added six points of opinion, saying that there are many points of reactionary suspicion. However, after examining the letters from Zhang Zhihui and others, there is no definite address. It is nothing more than anonymous letters. What is the basis for Director Miao's so-called reactionary suspicion? It is necessary to summon Director Miao to court for confrontation." Attorney Lu Xiangru stated, "The central government decided to apply the jury law to this case, but only for the sake of caution. In fact, Article 3 of the jury law is limited to cases that are returned or sent for a new trial. Since there is a legally promulgated jury law, the central government cannot change the law with the phrase 'apply the jury law system.' Please conclude this case as soon as possible in accordance with the law." Attorney Xu Bingcheng stated, "This case was reported by the Director of the Civil Affairs Department. It is necessary to summon Director Miao to court." Attorney Lu further stated, "Although the Civil Affairs Department has sent the original letters of Zhang Zhihui and others to the court, it has not disclosed their addresses. It is impossible to know whether these people exist. Even if they do, there is no way to summon them. Please pay attention." Attorney Wu Chengyu stated, "Under party rule, the power of the party is higher than the power of the government. Now the party committee appears in court as the defendant, which shows respect for the judiciary. Miao Bin, the former Director of the Civil Affairs Department, is the plaintiff, and he should also appear in court so that the case can be brought to light as soon as possible." He also said, "I have read three letters of evidence. Two of them have the same handwriting, and one was sent from Zhenjiang, but the signatory is more than two hundred citizens of Tongshan. Both of these points are suspicious. If it is considered necessary to adopt them, it is necessary to summon Director Miao to court."

Longhai Train Robbed at Bayiji

Xuzhou Correspondence: Bandits are rampant in eastern Xuzhou. The First Division has repeatedly sent teams to suppress them, and the bandits have dispersed separately. However, the bandits appear and disappear unpredictably, and gatherings and dissolutions are uncertain. Disturbances and robberies still occur from time to time. Yesterday (the 22nd), a train robbery occurred again on the eastern section of the ticket train at Bayiji Station. Fortunately, no one was injured and no roads were destroyed. In the morning of that day, the second ticket train from Haizhou to Xuzhou, with three third-class passenger cars and seven or eight freight cars, arrived at Bayiji Station at about 8:00 PM. At that time, a widow named So-and-so in Bayiji, because her son was abducted by bandits a month ago, and she entrusted someone to negotiate a price for redemption, transported dozens of stones of high-quality grain to Xuzhou for sale, hoping to obtain the money to redeem her son. She loaded the grain on the train at this station. Because loading the goods took time, the inspector escorting the train warned that the area was unsafe and that it was not advisable to stop for too long. However, before the goods were fully loaded, fifty or sixty bandits sneaked onto the train. First, one or two disguised bandits inquired if there were any military police escorting the train. The people at the station told them that there were none. The bandits did not pay attention to this and swarmed into the passenger cars, brandishing pistols and sharp blades, threatening the passengers not to make a sound and robbing them one by one. It is estimated that the fifty or sixty passengers lost about one thousand yuan in cash and about one thousand yuan in clothes and luggage. After the robbery, the bandits got off the train and fled. At that time, the people at the station were not aware of the incident, and the passengers were also panicked and afraid to make a sound. After the train started, the ticket inspector found out that the passengers had been robbed. The bandits had already fled far away. The train did not arrive at Xuzhou Station until 12:00 at night. It is said that one railway worker was fast asleep on the upper bunk in the carriage when the robbery occurred and was not seen by the bandits, so he was lucky enough to escape. It is said that the bandits were all in plain clothes and mostly spoke with a local accent. Fortunately, no roads were destroyed and no one was injured, otherwise the losses would have been even greater. (March 23rd)

Hunan Province Advocates National Goods Conference

Changsha Correspondence: In order to awaken the people to advocate national goods and resist foreign goods, the various circles of Hunan Province, initiated and convened by the Provincial Party Headquarters and the Provincial Government, gathered representatives from various agencies and groups to hold a meeting and decided to organize the Hunan People's National Goods Promotion Movement Committee. Huang Jing, Huang Yunlong, Yuan Zhang, and fifteen others were elected as organizers. A conference was held at the Provincial Education Association at 10:00 AM on the 23rd. More than 40,000 people attended. After performing the rituals, Chairman He Jian first reported the purpose of the meeting, saying that the national goods promotion movement is a national salvation movement. In other words, it means not buying foreign goods and using domestic goods. However, there are many domestic goods that cannot meet the demand, so we should all work together to focus on production. Food, clothing, housing, and transportation should all be able to meet the needs. Only then can the promotion of national goods be achieved. On the one hand, we should implement tariff autonomy and increase taxes on foreign goods so that domestic goods can be sold smoothly. Moreover, everyone should develop the habit of loving and using national goods and prevent leakage so that the country can become rich and strong. After He's report, more than ten people from various circles, including Tan Changkai, Zhang Kailian, and Zuo Yizhai, spoke one after another, generally advocating national goods negatively, actively setting up factories, and preventing the intrusion of foreign goods. Next, the chairman presented the conference's circular telegram and proposals and read them item by item, which were unanimously passed. Finally, the entire audience shouted slogans and dispersed. Subsequently, more than 240 propaganda teams from various agencies, groups, and schools carried propaganda materials and set off in four districts, east, west, south, and north, to carry out propaganda, which lasted until 6:00 PM. All stores and households posted slogans of "Promote National Goods" at their doors. The conference's circular telegram and proposals are recorded below: (Circular Telegram) "Since the end of the Qing Dynasty, the national power has declined, and the Eastern and Western powers have taken the opportunity to invade and oppress us heavily, causing great pain. Economic aggression is especially vicious. Sucking blood and marrow, the people are poor and the wealth is exhausted. This is a weapon that kills without bloodshed and is the only tool used by imperialists to destroy small and weak nations. Now, gold is expensive and silver is cheap, and foreign goods are expensive, which is a good opportunity to promote national goods. It is what the people of the whole country should actively strive for. I hope that all compatriots across the country will take advantage of this opportunity to revitalize industry, open up the natural wealth, and save the dying people's livelihood. The Party and the country are fortunate. The Hunan People's National Goods Promotion Movement Conference kowtows and prints." (Proposals) (1) Please ask the government to restore the paper mill and the labor suit factory. (2) Please ask the government to hold a product exhibition as soon as possible. (3) Please ask the government to issue a general order to reduce or exempt taxes on all domestic products. (4) Please ask the government party headquarters to order all public officials and party affairs workers to use domestic goods. (5) Please ask the Provincial Party Headquarters to strictly supervise merchants to promote the National Goods Association, continue its work, and implement the promotion of national goods. (6) Please ask the Party Headquarters to order merchant groups to organize a National Goods Evaluation Committee.

The North Manchurian Market Where the Powers Compete

With Britain, the United States, Japan, France, Russia, Germany, and Italy Investing the Most

Total Investment Has Reached Over 100 Million US Dollars

Harbin Correspondence: Manchuria is the Balkans of the East. A second world war is likely to break out due to the Manchurian problem. This is especially evident after the occurrence of the Chinese Eastern Railway problem. In recent years, the powers have focused their attention on Manchuria and have been investing in it in succession, becoming increasingly fierce. According to the latest foreign reports, the investment situation of various countries is as follows: (1) Soviet Russia: The total investment has reached 40 million US dollars, and the annual use of funds is about 75 million US dollars. (2) Japan: The total investment is 19.9 million yuan, and the annual use of funds is quite substantial. (3) Britain: British investment in enterprises totals 20 million US dollars, and the annual use of funds is about 51 million US dollars. In Harbin alone, there are as many as twenty-seven British enterprises. British merchants are very active. (4) United States: The commercial investment is about 4.5 million US dollars, and the use of funds far exceeds that of other countries, reaching 10 million US dollars per year. In the three northeastern provinces, there are twenty-six American commercial organizations. (5) Germany: There are twenty-two German commercial organizations, with a total investment of about 3 million US dollars and an annual use of funds of 8 million US dollars. (6) France: The total investment is 6 million US dollars, and the use of funds is 15 million US dollars. (7) Italy: Italy has no significant activities in Manchuria, but its investment has already reached 400,000 US dollars, which is a new investment in recent years. The use of funds has also reached 2 million US dollars. In the future, Italy's economic influence in northern Manchuria will be no less than that of other countries. (8) Other countries: The total investment has reached 1 million US dollars, and the use of funds is 7 million US dollars. (9) The total investment of White Russians has reached 11.25 million US dollars, surpassing the powers. However, it is feared that it will not be able to continue to develop in the future. Overall, foreign investment in Manchuria totals 11.25 million US dollars, and the annual use of funds reaches 400 million US dollars. Due to the increasing investment of the powers, the economic power of Chinese merchants is completely in the hands of foreigners, and the profits and losses of their businesses are all dependent on foreign merchants. It is very painful to talk about it.

Local Correspondence

Kunshan

Details of Lake Bandits' Looting of Zhangpu Town: Zhangpu Town in this county has always been an area where lake bandits frequently appear. On the 22nd, over 300 households and businesses in the entire town were completely looted by a large gang of two to three hundred lake bandits. The losses amounted to over 200,000 [currency unit]. Two people were killed, and 57 men, women, old, and young were kidnapped. The details of the looting at that time are recorded as follows: At 2:00 PM on the 23rd, more than ten large boats suddenly arrived at the South Great Bridge of the town. As the residents were still wondering, the bandits immediately gave an order. Over two hundred bandits rushed ashore, each with red cloth wrapped around their arms and holding small red flags, box cannons, pistols, machine guns, and rifles. They quickly set up sentry posts and separately attacked the security team and the public security bureau, seizing one box cannon and eight rifles. After seizing the firearms, the bandits went to the Seventh District Office, destroyed the telephone, and then searched and looted each household and business. All items of any value were completely looted. The looting ended at 6:00 PM. Before leaving, they fired a volley of shots, killing one farmer, Ma Sizhang, and one security team squad leader, Li Zengying. They kidnapped four security team members, one police officer, and 52 residents, including Chen Weizhang, Yi Yifan, Wen Xingqiao, Zeng Shixian, and Zeng Tangshi. They set sail from the North Great Bridge towards the Wusong River. The county water police team and the provincial water public security team received the report and rushed to suppress them, but the bandits had already fled far away. The county government sent a trial officer, Chen Ying, to conduct an investigation. Currently, Luo Xingwei of the district and Shen Guangdi, the director of the Public Security Sub-bureau, are handling the aftermath. None of the kidnapped people have been released yet.

Education News - Important News

Order from the Ministry of Education: Student Uniforms Should Use Domestic Goods

The Ministry of Education believes that student uniforms should be changed to use domestic goods. It has issued a special order to the Education Departments of various provinces and the Education Bureaus of special municipalities, stating: "The Central Executive Committee's Audit Office has sent an official letter stating, 'Recently, the Jiangsu Provincial Party Reorganization Committee has submitted a report (Committee Letter No. 4009) requesting that the National Schools be ordered to use domestic goods for student uniforms in the future in order to promote them.' It was approved by the Standing Committee and handed over to the Ministry of Education for review. A copy of the original report is attached. After investigation, it is clear that the materials for student uniforms in national schools must be completely domestic goods, as clearly stipulated in Article 7 of the Regulations on Student Uniforms issued by the Ministry. Now, according to the previous reason, the previous order should be reiterated to promote this. In addition to replying to the letter, the original attachment is hereby copied and sent for compliance. The affiliated organizations are also instructed to comply and report the handling situation for verification. This order."

Ministry of Education Issues Order to Change School Holidays

Implementing in the 19th Year... Abolishing the Lunar New Year Winter Vacation

The Ministry of Education, in order to abolish the Lunar New Year winter vacation, revise the school year and semester system, and the regulations on holiday dates, has issued an order to the education departments of each province, universities, and special municipality education bureaus, stating:

Regarding the previous approval by this Ministry of the Secretariat of the Central Executive Committee's Document No. 1647, recently received from the Standing Committee the presentation from the Hebei Provincial Party Affairs Reorganization Committee, which forwarded a request from the Changping County Steering Committee to order all schools nationwide to abolish the Lunar New Year winter vacation and implement the National Calendar New Year holiday, which was approved "to be forwarded to the Ministry of Education." A copy of the original presentation is enclosed for your review, and an additional copy is submitted to this Ministry. Considering that our country is vast, with varying climates, the southern regions are close to the tropics, naturally free from severe winter cold, while in the northern regions, the cold season begins in late autumn and continues until early summer. Even in the central regions, due to differences in latitude, mountains, seas, and plains, the start and end of the cold season vary from place to place. Even if schools must take a break due to severe cold, there is no reason for them to all be during the Lunar December and January. Therefore, the so-called winter vacation is actually using the name of "winter vacation" to preserve the custom of celebrating the Lunar New Year. At a time when the National Government is clearly ordering the implementation of the National Calendar, it is inappropriate to allow this practice to continue. This is the first reason why it should be abolished immediately. The name "winter vacation" is a false pretext, and its dates often shift with the Lunar New Year festivals. As a result, the length of the first and second semesters in each school year varies, and the corresponding semesters in different school years also differ in the number of days. Due to this, the curriculum of the first and second semesters in each school year cannot be evenly distributed, and the number of teaching days and the amount of content in the corresponding semesters of each school year cannot be made equal. This harms school education deeply. To remedy these issues, it is even more inappropriate to allow this practice to continue. This is the second reason why it should be abolished immediately. Furthermore, the ban on recording the Lunar Calendar in almanacs has been repeatedly ordered by the National Government for compliance. From now on, there will be no reliable basis for checking Lunar New Year festivals. Even if private individuals secretly use the old methods, making reckless calculations and spreading them in violation of the ban, their errors will be obvious. These Lunar New Year festivals are already baseless, and the winter vacation associated with them cannot be preserved. This is the third reason why it should be abolished immediately. This Ministry, in accordance with the National Government's repeated orders to implement the National Calendar and prohibit the use of the Lunar Calendar, and also adopting the intention of the original presentation from the Hebei Provincial Party Affairs Reorganization Committee, has decided to abolish the winter vacation, which has been a major obstacle to school education for more than ten years. Starting from the 11th year of the Republic (1922), all schools nationwide must not have winter vacations. However, considering that the beginning of reform should embody both the transformation of customs and the retention of habitual practices, the National Calendar New Year holiday will be extended to three weeks, allowing the general public to transfer all kinds of customs associated with the Lunar New Year's end and beginning, such as sacrifices, celebrations, banquets, entertainment, and rest, to this New Year holiday period. Teachers, staff and students of all levels of schools should be models and advocates to promote the National Calendar. In addition to replying to the Secretariat of the Central Executive Committee and requesting them to review and forward this matter, the Regulations on the School Year, Semester, and Holiday Dates have been revised and submitted to the Executive Yuan for review, and then submitted to the National Government for approval and record. Subsequently, Instruction No. 741 from the Executive Yuan was received, stating that the submission and attachments had been reviewed. The Ministry's proposal to abolish the winter vacation related to the Lunar New Year festivals in all schools nationwide starting from the 19th year (1930), and to extend the New Year holiday period, is in line with the purpose of promoting the National Calendar and should be approved. The revised Regulations on the School Year, Semester, and Holiday Dates should be promulgated by ministerial order for implementation, and then reported to the National Government for review and record. Furthermore, Instruction No. 983 from the Executive Yuan was received, stating that the previous submission from the Ministry regarding the abolishment of the winter vacation, extension of the New Year holiday, and revision of the Regulations on the School Year, Semester, and Holiday Dates, which was submitted to the Yuan for review, has been forwarded for review and instructions have been issued. Now, Instruction No. 467 from the National Government has been received, stating, "All submissions have been reviewed and approved for record. The documents are stored," etc. Therefore, it is hereby ordered for your information. Accordingly, this Ministry will immediately promulgate the revised Regulations on the School Year, Semester, and Holiday Dates, and it will take effect from August 1, 1930. From the 19th school year onwards, all schools nationwide should comply with these regulations and must not have winter vacations. The school calendar for the 19th school year for schools at all levels should be compiled separately by the respective "Departments," "Schools," and "Bureaus" according to the provisions of Article 10, Paragraph 1 of these regulations by May 31 of this year, and reported directly or forwarded to this Ministry for approval. In addition to promulgation and separate orders, a copy of the revised Regulations on School Year, Semester, and Holiday Dates is hereby issued for the "Departments," "Schools," and "Bureaus" to comply with and instruct their subordinates to comply with. This order,

Including the attached revised Regulations on School Year, Semester, and Holiday Dates, one copy.

Regulations on School Year, Semester, and Holiday Dates

Article 1: The school year for all levels of schools begins on August 1 of each year and ends on July 31 of the following year.

Article 2: One school year is divided into two semesters: August 1 to January 31 of the following year is the first semester, and February 1 to July 31 is the second semester.

Article 3: All levels of schools will designate several days within the week following the start of the second semester as a period for the new semester to begin. During this period, classes may be temporarily suspended to complete the administrative tasks of the previous semester and handle matters such as student enrollment for the current semester. However, the number of days must not exceed the following limits:

Universities and colleges: 7 days,

Secondary schools: 5 days,

Elementary schools: 3 days.

During the period for the new semester to begin, all levels of schools may, depending on the circumstances, implement career guidance, further education guidance, course selection guidance, etc. The principal may designate teachers or specially invite external personnel to take charge of these tasks, and students may be encouraged to engage in various extracurricular activities beneficial to their physical and mental well-being. During the period for the new semester to begin, students should attend school unless they are transferring to another school, pursuing further education, or have unavoidable circumstances and have been granted leave by the school. Those who violate this rule will be considered absent.

Article 4: Except for the temporary suspension of classes during the period for the new semester to begin as specified in Article 3 and the Category A holidays specified in Article 5, the number of days in the school term for each level of school shall be as follows:

Universities and colleges: 132 days per semester,

Secondary schools: 140 days per semester,

Elementary schools: 144 days per semester.

The number of days occupied by each month and the start and end dates are as shown in Appendix (A).

Article 5: The holiday dates for all levels of schools each year are as follows:

(A) Regular Holidays:

(1) Universities and colleges: limited to 70 days, secondary schools: limited to 56 days, elementary schools: limited to 50 days, (2) New Year holidays: all levels of schools are uniformly limited to 21 days, (3) Spring Break: all levels of schools are uniformly set at 3 days.

(B) Commemorative Holidays:

(1) Confucius' Birthday Memorial (August 27 of the National Calendar), (2) National Day Memorial (October 10 of the National Calendar), (3) Dr. Sun Yat-sen's Birthday Memorial (November 12 of the National Calendar), (4) Founding of the Republic of China Memorial (January 1 of the National Calendar), (5) Dr. Sun Yat-sen's Death Memorial (March 12 of the National Calendar), (6) Huanghuagang Seventy-Two Martyrs' Memorial (March 29 of the National Calendar), (7) National Revolutionary Army Inauguration Memorial (July 9 of the National Calendar).

All levels of schools should have a day off for each of the above commemorative days, and hold commemorative ceremonies and speeches on that day.

Article 6: The start and end dates of the Category A holidays in the preceding article are as specified in Appendix (B).

Article 7: Special local commemorative days for which holidays should be granted must be approved by the education departments of each province or the education bureaus of each special municipality and reported to the Ministry of Education for record.

Article 8: The number of school anniversary holidays for each level of school shall not exceed two days per year.

Article 9: In addition to Sundays and various class suspensions and holiday dates specified in Articles 3, 5, 7, and 8, holidays shall not be taken arbitrarily. Various gatherings should be held on Sundays. The measures for national humiliation memorials will be determined separately.

Article 10: The school calendar for universities and colleges should be compiled by each school based on these regulations two months before the start of the school year and reported directly or forwarded to the Ministry of Education for approval. The school calendar for secondary schools and below should be formulated and promulgated by the education departments of each province or the education bureaus of each special municipality based on these regulations two months before the start of the school year and reported to the Ministry of Education for record. Secondary schools and below attached to national or private universities and colleges, and secondary schools and below established by various agencies of the National Government in various provinces and special municipalities, should comply with the school calendar formulated and promulgated by the education department or education bureau of the location where they are located. The same applies to secondary schools and below attached to provincial universities and colleges in each province or secondary schools and below attached to provincial universities and colleges in each province located within the boundaries of special municipalities.

Article 11: The start and end dates of the summer vacation may be appropriately adjusted (such as advanced or delayed) for rural elementary schools with special circumstances, according to the local agricultural conditions. The vacation may also be divided into several sections for intermittent vacations (such as separate silkworm, wheat, and autumn harvest vacations to reduce the summer vacation dates). However, the total number of vacation days must not exceed the limit of 50 days and must be approved by the education department of each province or the education bureau of the special municipality.

Article 13: These regulations will take effect on August 1, 1930.

(Explanation) All levels of schools should resume classes from January 11 to January 31 after the end of the New Year holiday, 21 days, to conclude the curriculum of the first semester and hold semester exams. After the end of the first semester, the school administration should finish affairs relating to the first semester during the semester transition period, and handle issues such as enrolling transfer students, and students who are joining mid-semester, so that the students are able to transfer or continue their studies during this semester. Without necessary situations, those approved by the governing educational authorities, and students may transfer schools during this semester. It is not permissible to hold semester exams in advance before the New Year holiday. Even schools that are approved to hold semester exams in advance should still resume classes for 21 days after the end of the New Year holiday.

Local News

The Municipal Education Bureau Formulates Measures for the Tutor System

Order for Implementation in Municipal Middle Schools

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau, recognizing that the implementation of a tutor system in schools allows teachers to fulfill their guidance responsibilities outside of class and students to learn the principles of self-cultivation and social interaction in addition to their studies, is highly effective in fostering and developing students' individuality. Therefore, it has formulated sixteen articles for implementation and issued them to all municipal secondary schools yesterday for compliance. The main points of the Measures for Implementing the Tutor System in Municipal Secondary Schools are excerpted as follows: (1) The purpose of the tutor system is to enable teachers and students to live together, understand students' individualities, develop the virtues of the five educations, cultivate the virtues of dealing with people, and provide guidance on all aspects of life. (2) Tutors in each school shall be nominated from the teaching staff by the school affairs meeting. (3) Each tutor shall guide ten to fifteen students. (4) Tutors for the first, second, and third grades of junior high school and the first grade of senior high school shall be designated by the moral education meeting. Senior high school students in the second and third grades may choose their tutors freely. (5) For the free selection of tutors, students shall fill out a tutor selection form with the tutor of their first choice to a certain number of choices. Each choice should list one tutor. Tutors shall be assigned according to the order in which the forms are submitted. If the first choice tutor is already full, the student should choose their second choice, and so on. (6) Once a tutor has been designated or selected, they may not be changed mid-term, except in special circumstances and with the approval of the moral education meeting. (7) Those who hold outside positions or teach more than six hours per week shall not be eligible to serve as tutors. (8) All tutors must reside at the school. (9) If there are insufficient tutors, the system shall be implemented in the highest or lowest classes of junior and senior high school as much as possible. (10) The designation or selection of tutors shall be held once per semester, and the allocation of tutors shall be completed by the third week of the semester. (11) Tutors shall hold a group meeting with all their students at least once per week, and individual meetings may be held at any time. (12) All tutors in each school shall meet once a month to discuss matters that should be promoted or reformed, and submit them to the moral education meeting for approval and implementation. (13) Once a tutor has been selected or designated, they may not resign on frivolous grounds. In case of unavoidable circumstances, the matter must be submitted to the school affairs meeting for decision. (14) Tutors shall submit a monthly report on their work to the principal. (15) Each school shall report on the implementation of the tutor system to the bureau once per semester. (16) These measures shall be implemented after being approved by the bureau affairs meeting.

Municipal Education Bureau Dispatches Personnel to Thoroughly Investigate the Complaint Against Jiannan Middle School

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau dispatched personnel to thoroughly investigate the complaint against Jiannan Middle School. According to the report, "Regarding the report, we were ordered to thoroughly investigate the case of Jiannan Middle School being accused of being a communist training organization. We complied and went to the school located at 33 Maigen Road at 1 PM on the 24th of this month to investigate. Because the school was located in a remote area, we had to ask around several times before we finally saw the so-called Jiannan Middle School. There was no school sign at the intersection, only a sign that read 'Jiannan Middle School First Institute' hanging at the entrance. We entered and asked to see the principal, but were told that he was not at the school. We then inspected the school building, which was a four-story residential house. There were three rooms on one side of the ground floor, and a staircase on the other side. The doors of the rooms were open, and there were two people who looked like students reading newspapers. We asked them if the principal was at the school, and they pointed to an inner room. We saw a man in a suit and glasses pacing back and forth. We asked him his name, and he said that he was the principal, Fang Jirui. We then talked about the school's past and present situation. He made the following remarks: 'I was entrusted by important figures of the Party and the country to found this school. The school board members are He Jian, Lu Dipin, Lin Zhiyu, Zhu Hegeng, Zhuang Xiquan, Cao Wanshun, Yi Shunyu, Zhang Ji and others. The Director of Studies is Ms. Zheng Yongtao, a Sichuan native. The other faculty and staff have not yet been finalized. Our school just opened this month. The school is divided into two parts. This place is for classrooms, offices, female dormitories, and the female cafeteria. The other part is at 36 Wuding Road, which serves as the male dormitory and the senior high school second grade classroom. There are more than one hundred students in total, with females accounting for more than ten. Our school has already submitted an application for registration in accordance with the Shanghai Private School Regulations, and my friends are familiar with Director Chen of the Municipal Education Bureau, so this matter should not be a problem.' After the conversation, we inspected the school building. The ground floor office was decorated with desks and filing cabinets. The female cafeteria had two square tables and several long benches. One room on the second floor was supposed to be a library, but it was currently empty. It was said that the school was just founded and was waiting for donations. There were two classrooms with desks and chairs made of unfinished wood. Each room had about eleven or twelve sets. There were words 'Pujiang Middle School' written on the drawers with white chalk. We do not know whether they were purchased from that school or were reorganized. There were also two classrooms on the third floor, all very simply furnished. While we were visiting, a female student was playing the organ, and two other female students came down from upstairs. There was a piece of paper pasted on the wall, which read 'Female Dormitory', so we did not go upstairs to visit. We then left the school and went to the school's dormitory on Wuding Road. The building had four floors, which were single rooms. One room on the second floor was a classroom, and the rest were used as bedrooms. Regarding the accused counter-revolutionary organization, we were unable to search the students' rooms for fear of misunderstanding, and the location in the concession made it even more difficult. The principal said that there were more than one hundred students, but we only saw seven or eight. We only saw the principal and the director of studies. We arrived at the school at about 2:15 PM, but there was not a single person in the classroom, which was quite strange. It is now the end of March and the school just opened. According to the explicit order of the Ministry of Education on February 1, the school must first apply for establishment before it can enroll students. The school has not complied with the law, which is not in compliance with regulations. According to the school's prospectus, the academic system is divided into arts and sciences. The arts subjects can be used as a facade, but the science subjects have no equipment at all. Furthermore, the school is enrolling transfer students for the first and second grades of senior high school and all grades of junior high school. If junior high school students study for three months, they can obtain a junior high school diploma. Newly opened schools enrolling transfer students like this are suspicious of being insubstantial. Chen Wenbin's letter accused the school of training party members and organizing demonstrations and factory strikes. It was difficult to find out by asking the school authorities and students. We fear that they would not dare to reveal the truth for fear of being caught by the law. It seems that the municipal party headquarters should conduct a secret investigation to clarify the matter. We hereby report the facts truthfully to you for your consideration. Respectfully submitted to Director Chen."

The entire team of over a hundred people will leave Shanghai for Hangzhou on the 29th. Guangdong women's basketball has traditionally used men's rules. Recently, because the National Games adopted a two-zone system for women's rules, it has been quite disadvantageous to the Guangdong team. They have been training in women's techniques recently, under the guidance of Mr. Wei Zesheng. The team has average talent and is very lively. They are especially confident in their shooting skills. As for the men's volleyball team, they are not only vying for the Far Eastern representation but also harbor a sense of revenge. They are bound to have a fierce battle at the National Games. Observing the strength of the Guangdong team, they are very solid, and their tactics are quite ingenious. The person on the left side of the first row is especially fierce. In short, the team has uncanny passing skills and unpredictable spiking skills. Their saving skills are also very steady. It is hoped that the Shanghai team will pay attention to this.

(2) Liaoning Not Going to Hangzhou Today

The entire team is still staying at the Zhenhua Hotel. They will not leave Shanghai today. Among them, the women's volleyball team is quite strong. The men's group has about twenty people, and their methods are purely German. This is because the team's instructor is the German, Mr. Bochen. They do not rotate when throwing the discus. This method is fine for tall people, but it may not be suitable for short people. In running, they alternate between using their heels and toes. For example, in the 100-meter race, they use their heels for 50 meters and their toes for 50 meters. This method seems to have some rationale.

A Scene from the Jiangnan University Basketball Game

Yesterday (the 22nd), the two Jiangnan University basketball teams, Groups A and B, went to Zhizhi University on Jiangwan Road to compete with the university's basketball team for the Jiangnan University basketball championship. The Group B teams from the two schools started the game at 2:30 PM. In the beginning, the strengths of the two sides were relatively equal. Falling behind, Jiangnan University gradually could not support Zhizhi University's defense, with Wei Kongguangyi coming and going to resist. Jiangnan University Group B could not fight back. In the first half, Zhizhi University Group B took the lead with a score of 33 to 10. The final result was that Zhizhi University Group B won with a score of 60 to 20. The referee was Shao Ji. At 3:30 PM, the Group A teams from the two schools began contact. Zhizhi University relied on the psychology of a larger number of people, all thinking that Jiangnan University was no match for them. Unexpectedly, after 40 minutes of struggle, Jiangnan University Group A won with a score of 49 to 43. The first half was 24 to 19, with Jiangnan University in the lead. The referee was still Shao Ji.

Local News

City Propaganda Department Preparing for Huanghuagang Commemoration

Announcing Commemoration Measures

The 29th of this month is the memorial day for the tragic and painful martyrdom of the 72 martyrs of Huanghuagang. Tracing back its historical outline, it was two years before the founding of the Republic of China. After the ninth failure of our party in Guangzhou, Huang Keqiang, Zhao Sheng, and others gathered the elite revolutionary parties from various provinces in Guangzhou. One year before the founding of the Republic of China (i.e., 1911 in the Western calendar during the reign of Emperor Xuantong of the Qing Dynasty), on March 29th, they launched another uprising, attacking and burning the Governor's Office. Those who died in battle and were killed totaled 72 people, all buried collectively at Huanghuagang, hence the name "72 Martyrs of Huanghuagang." It was also decided that this day would be the memorial day for this tragic incident. The city's propaganda department has formulated measures and is actively preparing for a grand memorial ceremony to express condolences and honor the loyal martyrs. It is said that on the morning of that day, representatives from various agencies, groups, and party departments at all levels will be convened at the Tai Li Hall of the City Party Headquarters on LinYin Road in the South City. Four representatives from each will participate to jointly hold a memorial service. The City Executive Committee will also notify all sectors to uniformly comply with the following five commemorative measures: (1) Holiday for one day, (2) Half-mast for one day, (3) Citywide silence for five minutes at noon (signaled by naval gun salutes), (4) Suspension of entertainment banquets for one day, (5) All civil servants and party members in the city to wear black armbands for one day (to be prepared by themselves). It is imagined that there will be a tragic and enthusiastic atmosphere at that time. The entire commemorative measures formulated by the City Propaganda Department are attached below so as to clarify the whole picture of the commemorative matters: A. Commemorative aspects: (1) At 9:00 AM on March 29th, convene four representatives from party departments at all levels, various agencies, mass organizations, and schools, as well as all party members, at the City Party Headquarters to hold a memorial service. (2) The City Party Headquarters will notify all sectors of the city: 1. Holiday for one day, 2. Half-mast for one day, 3. Citywide silence for five minutes at noon (signaled by naval gun salutes), 4. Suspension of entertainment banquets for one day, 5. All civil servants and party members in the city to wear black armbands for one day (black armbands to be prepared by themselves). (3) Zhenru, Meilong, Pudong, Jiangwan, Wusong, and other districts will hold separate memorial services. Other commemorative aspects should comply with the regulations stipulated in these measures. (4) In addition to participating in the memorial service convened by this department, all sectors may separately handle the regulations stipulated in these measures. (5) All newspapers will print the portrait and will of the Premier on the front page, and print them in blue. B. Propaganda aspects: A. Propaganda outline: (1) According to the regulations for commemorative ceremonies for revolutionary memorial days, (2) According to the propaganda outline and key points issued by this department, (3) Expose the betrayal and crimes of the Northern warlord Yan Xishan against the party and the country, (4) Support the Central Government and the policy of realizing peaceful reunification, (5) Support Chairman Chiang, who has made great contributions to the country, (6) Implement all resolutions of the Third Plenary Session of the Central Committee. B. Propaganda materials: (1) Propaganda outline, (2) Propaganda key points, (3) Leaflets, (4) Slogans, (5) Special issue of the Party Voice, (6) Special issues of publications in various districts, (7) Compile a commemorative album, (8) Compile a biography of the 72 martyrs, (9) Write a letter to comrades (City Training Department), write a letter to the masses (City Civil Training Association). C. Propaganda methods: (1) Party departments at all levels and permanent propaganda teams will set off to give lectures, (2) Widely post slogans, (3) Airplanes or cars will distribute small slogans, (4) Distribute leaflets, (5) Others.

Hai Rong Battleship Returned to Shanghai Yesterday

Commander-in-Chief Chiang Still in Fenghua

The Hai Rong warship that Commander-in-Chief Chiang took to his hometown to sweep the tombs returned to Songkou early yesterday morning to add coal. The Jiankang warship that accompanied him is still in Ningbo's Li Port. As of noon yesterday, Chiang had not yet left Fenghua. Chen Shaokuan, the Vice Minister of Naval Affairs, is also said to be with Chiang in Fenghua.

Heavy Fog Outside Wusong Blocks Ships

The Fengtian Maru Arrived Late The Dalian Steamship Company's Fengtian Maru ship, this time coming from Dalian via Qingdao to Shanghai, was originally scheduled to enter the port yesterday. Some of the Northeast athletes participating in the Zhejiang National Games were on board the ship to Shanghai, transferring to Hangzhou. However, the ship suddenly encountered heavy fog on the night of the 24th when it sailed to Sanjiaoshui, and the ship's route was obscured by the fog and could not be distinguished. In order to ensure safe navigation, the captain ordered the ship to anchor at sea and wait for the fog to dissipate before continuing. As a result, it did not arrive in Shanghai yesterday and will have to arrive this morning. The passengers were stranded on the ship for a day before arriving in Shanghai.

American Mail Ship Delayed The American Mail Steamship Company's Pacific mail ship, the Jefferson, coming from the United States to Shanghai, was scheduled to enter the port yesterday morning as usual. When it reached the outside of Wusong, about fifty nautical miles away, the route was obscured by fog. Fearing danger, the captain anchored there, intending to enter the port after the fog cleared. By yesterday afternoon, the ship was also constrained by the receding tide and could not move, so it could not sail in. It sent a radio message to Shanghai, saying that it would wait for the tide to rise before it could leave the shallows and sail to Shanghai, which is expected to be today. The ships leaving Shanghai that were blocked by fog outside Wusong were only able to go to sea one after another at noon yesterday.

Timber Ship Sunk The commercial ship Beringham, which was transporting timber from North America to the Far East, was loaded with a full ship of timber and sailed to China and Little Luzon to unload. When it reached the Fangzhou Strait outside Yokohama, Japan, it encountered wind and fog, and the stern of the ship struck a reef. The rear hold was ruptured, the rudder machine and leaves fell off, and seawater entered the hold, causing the ship to sink. It is said that the crew and sailors have already been rescued to Japan by a rescue ship sent from Yokohama, while the ship and cargo were completely lost.

Shipping News

Sharp Decrease in Northern Cargo The situation in the North is gradually becoming tense. The Tianjin shipping group has sent a telegram to Shanghai, ordering a reduction in cargo handling from today. Shanghai originally had a large amount of miscellaneous grain to be shipped to Tianjin, but shipments have been suspended recently. Even the goods ordered by foreign merchants that are transferred from Shanghai to Tianjin have been instructed by telegram to be stored in Shanghai from this week. In the past two days, the export cargo of each ship going to Tianjin has only been 20-30%. However, passenger traffic has increased because the Jinpu Railway is blocked, and many people have changed to sea routes. All ships coming and going are crowded with passengers, and ticket prices on all ships have also increased.

Inspection of Incoming and Outgoing Passengers The Shanghai Customs was ordered to inspect passengers on incoming and outgoing commercial ships. The original order required ships entering and leaving the port to anchor at the mouth of Wusong to wait for customs officials to board the ship for inspection. After the Shanghai shipping companies requested that this be waived, because the Wusong tide is high and the water is rapid, anchoring and waiting for inspection often causes ships to collide with each other or be washed aground by the tide, which is dangerous. The Customs did not agree. It is now reported that the matter has been discussed and a result has been reached: the commercial ships are now ordered to anchor in the Wusong Yuncao Port and wait for customs officials to inspect them. This is convenient for both the public and private sectors and there is no danger of accidents. The inspection will be implemented immediately.

Kuae Lee Returns to Shanghai for Repairs The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's Kuae Lee ship was attacked by bandits with cannons and gunfire in Majiazhai on the upper reaches of the Yangtze River. Fortunately, the crew was not injured, as reported in yesterday's newspaper. The ship has now telegraphed that it will return to Shanghai from Shashi to specially install steel plates to protect the drivers and passengers from bullets. The bandits in various places on the upper reaches of the Yangtze River are elusive, and it is very dangerous to travel by ship. It is difficult to travel without installing steel plates.

Shigemitsu Aoi's Mission to Beijing Last Night

Exchanging Notifications on the Reorganization of the Provisional Court

Japan Has Unconditionally Recognized the Reorganization

Japanese Acting Minister Shigemitsu Aoi went to Beijing last week. Because Ambassador Adachi came to Shanghai, he hurriedly returned to Shanghai, staying in Beijing for only one day and unable to fully negotiate various matters. Yesterday (the 25th), he went to Beijing at 11:00 PM, accompanied by Secretary Lin Chu, at the invitation of Foreign Minister Wang. He will stay in Beijing for three days and is scheduled to return to Shanghai on the night train on the 29th. As for the mission to Beijing this time, in addition to handling routine diplomatic affairs, he will also exchange notifications with the Ministry of Foreign Affairs on the reorganization of the Shanghai Provisional Court. Japan has unconditionally recognized the reorganization of the Provisional Court. In order to comply with diplomatic practice, he specially went to Beijing to exchange notifications. The reorganization of the Provisional Court was decided by a conference of six countries convened by the National Government. Japan, as a non-treaty country, did not participate. Now, because the effective date is approaching on April 1, Japan is inconvenient to act differently. Also, because the Sino-Japanese Tariff Agreement has been drafted, the positions of China and Japan are different from before. After several informal consultations between Foreign Minister Wang and Acting Minister Shigemitsu Aoi, a final solution was reached. Japan then automatically and unconditionally recognized the reorganization of the Provisional Court.

During the period of the National Games and the incense market, it is probably impossible not to reserve in advance. (10) Please inform us of the date of arrival in Hangzhou so that we can welcome you.
